  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_23457fca-ea5c-4d20-a22c-6880dae3dbc2'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/573156318?book_show_action=true">Mar 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer573156318" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12703399809800671078">3.5 ★'s<br/><br/>This is the last book in the Forever trilogy about Ellery and Connor Black.<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Likes:</u>
</b><br/><br/>• Lots of sexy time!<br/><br/>• I enjoyed how Conner and Ellery were learning about each other and growing as a couple.<br/><br/>• Julia!<br/><br/>• "Mysterious guy"...even if it was easy to figure out!<br/><br/>• Connor ending up at Club S...I like how it brought things full circle.<br/><br/>• Collin...that was a nice touch.<br/><br/>• The epilogue.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387786063i/7670329.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Dislikes:</u>
</b><br/><br/>• Lots of sexy time...it was a bit of an overkill!<br/><br/>• I enjoyed how Conner and Ellery were learning about</span>
  <span id="freeText12703399809800671078" style="display:none">3.5 ★'s<br><br>This is the last book in the Forever trilogy about Ellery and Connor Black.<br><br><b>
  <u>Likes:</u>
</b><br><br>• Lots of sexy time!<br><br>• I enjoyed how Conner and Ellery were learning about each other and growing as a couple.<br><br>• Julia!<br><br>• "Mysterious guy"...even if it was easy to figure out!<br><br>• Connor ending up at Club S...I like how it brought things full circle.<br><br>• Collin...that was a nice touch.<br><br>• The epilogue.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387786063i/7670329.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <u>Dislikes:</u>
</b><br><br>• Lots of sexy time...it was a bit of an overkill!<br><br>• I enjoyed how Conner and Ellery were learning about each other and growing as a couple but...they seemed to make the same mistake over and over.<br><br>• All the 'contrived' dramas...it was never ending! <br><br><br><b>
  <u>Overall:</u>
</b><br><br>I think it's a good book that wraps up the series nicely. I probably would've liked it more if the dramas focused more on them learning and dealing with becoming a family. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383701509i/6637626.jpg" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ “Is that so? What if I don’t want you to make love to me?” <br><br>“Ellery Rose Black! I better never hear those words come from your mouth.”<br><br>♥ “You’re the light in my life and when you’re not around, my world is dark. I will never do anything to jeopardize our relationship again. I make this promise to you, Ellery Black, that from this day forward, I will never keep anything from you. You have my word, baby. I promise forever.”<br><br>♥ “I’m so in love with you, and I need you. I need you every day. You’re my strength and my light and, without you, I’m nothing.”<br><br>♥ "You’re my infinity, Mr. Black.” <br><br>I turned to her and smiled as I traced her lips with my finger before brushing mine against them. “Forever us, baby. It’ll always be forever us.”</span>
  <a data-text-id="12703399809800671078" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17430850794740296726"><b> 5 Forever Us Stars </b><br/><br/>I thought this book was magnificent. What a way to finish a series/trilogy. We truly got to see how Conner and Ellery's life turned out. I have loved both of these characters since the beginning. Conner and Ellery were just such strong characters. Yes they both had jealousy and trust issues at times but as a couple you could just feel the love and connection between them.   <span id="freeText17430850794740296726" style="display:none"><b> 5 Forever Us Stars </b><br /><br />I thought this book was magnificent. What a way to finish a series/trilogy. We truly got to see how Conner and Ellery's life turned out. I have loved both of these characters since the beginning. Conner and Ellery were just such strong characters. Yes they both had jealousy and trust issues at times but as a couple you could just feel the love and connection between them. I thought this book was great, not only did we get to see how Conner and Ellery end up the author created some new twists and drama to keep us turning the page. Plus she also gave us an ending to the Ashlyn storyline. I was happy to see how that worked out. We also got to see an emotional side to the characters when something happens to someone very close to both of them.<br /><br />I would definitely recommend this book to anyone who is a fan of the author or has read the other two books in this trilogy. You really don't want to miss this book. It totally brings Conner and Ellery's story full circle. It also sets up for the next novella that is being released in December....Being Julia. I excited to read about her story and see more of Mr. and Mrs. Black.</span>

<div id="review_696930796" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/696930796" />
    <a title="Francine Lou" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19648038-francine-lou"><img alt="Francine Lou" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1390602850p2/19648038.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/696930796?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Francine Lou" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Francine Lou" href="/user/show/19648038-francine-lou">Francine Lou</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19648038-francine-lou?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer696930796" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2298850471577854293">I loved this last book of the forever trilogy ! There is a feeling of being complete reading Connor and Ellery continuing their life with a new baby and tackling life's challenges along with their life changing event! It was great to feel how much they loved one another and got through so much ! Connor and Ellery made me laugh so many times in this book as the first book made me cry more than laugh. I also loved Denny as he was such a great father figure and hilarious at times ! Wait until you h</span>
  <span id="freeText2298850471577854293" style="display:none">I loved this last book of the forever trilogy ! There is a feeling of being complete reading Connor and Ellery continuing their life with a new baby and tackling life's challenges along with their life changing event! It was great to feel how much they loved one another and got through so much ! Connor and Ellery made me laugh so many times in this book as the first book made me cry more than laugh. I also loved Denny as he was such a great father figure and hilarious at times ! Wait until you hit the scene of the hotel with the party where it was so intense that I was basically screaming and my blood pressure must have risen as I was so anxious and tense! All that kept coming out of my mouth was NNNNNNNOOOOOOOO!!!! OMG..OMG...!!!!! The author have such a surprise and she did an excellent job in that scene ! I almost collapsed finishing that scene in relief! The author played that scene so well!!! I hated to see their story ending and loved every bit of it!!! They complete and love each other forever!</span>

Connor Black is just so mmm....mmm.mmmm...lickable. <br/><br/>I have w</span>
  <span id="freeText15478262086895565731" style="display:none">Oh wow. Where to start. Well if you love theses stories as much as I do then you know how hard it is to find the exact words to portray the feelings you feel when you read them. I will stay the first story I cried, yes I did I cried like a baby. That one ripped my heart out. The next well I cried a little but nothing like the first but these stories twist you up in knots but and getting you so wound up. It's exhilarating and consuming. Connor Black is just so mmm....mmm.mmmm...lickable. <br /><br />I have waited for this story after the cliffhanger from the last and I ore ordered and waited until late so I could begin my adventure and it was so worth it. It was worth the wait, the anxiety and the sleep deprevation. Ellery and Connor or just a force to be reckoned with. They clash, because they both are so hard headed but it's so addicting to read about the two. You can feel the love they have for one another it overpowers everything. Even their arguments have you all tripped up because you know that Connor is going to make it up to her and it's going to be hot! <br /><br />I've always loved the characters in these stories they are so well written and such big parts in the lives of Connor and Ellery. <br /><br /><br />I must say when Ellery was in labor I was so nervous. I could feel the nervous energy that Conor was feeling and I wanted to wrap my arms around him all the while I wanted to hold Ellery's hand. <br /><br />What amazing parents they both are, it was just heart melting to watch them both interact with Julia. There were parts where you once again felt the angst, and nervousness settle in and I will say at one part the author had me. I was like wth, what's going on no way can this happen that's just not Ellery and when I finally got to the bottom of it I was thinking well played and laughed. <br /><br />The entires story was awesome. You get to once again enjoy the lives if Mr. And Mrs. Black. We get to go on the journey of parenthood and marriage, the good moments the bad and the sad. <br /><br />The author did an amazing job and I loved the ending. My heart is full and happy.<br /><br />Kudos on another amazing book!!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15478262086895565731" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

I can not say how much I loved this trilogy and this final book to get the complete picture of the Blacks family and their friends life. Thank you Sandi Lynn.   <span id="freeText1979668653224552766" style="display:none">This was a beautiful ending to a fantastic story, They really went through a lot of drama, but loive came thrtpugh it all.<br /><br />They were so good together, and so bad. Their friends were brilliant, always there when they were needed. Denny was such a sweetie, it was really sad when he got ill. but was really happy when he started on the roads to recovery.<br /><br />Their love was just as passionate all the way through, and Connor didn't always do the right things, he made some big mistakes kept secrets almost causing him bigger problems. I loved how they came together and made up after their fights.<br /><br />Mason was a perfect mannie, absolutely loved Julia, he seemed such a natural with her. I was thrilled when he moved to NYC. <br /><br />The trial took its toll on them both, unfortunately keeping things away from each other, for as much as they loved each other, they really went hard at hurting each other with lies and secrets, I was team Ellery all the way, Ashlyn deserved all she got,<br /><br />Then Ellery is being stalked, horrible words! and Connor doesn't. disappoint he let's his temper win over causing more problems. They eventually get that sorted put, but Connor tackles it wrong again, causing him the biggest nightmare, he did his usual coping mechanism and drank himself silly, it was a sweet union and i was really pleased they made up,<br /><br />I loved the epilogue! perfect ending! so sweet Julia had her daddy wrapped around her finger, and how perfect when another little baby made its appearance.<br /><br />The final part was beautiful, really summed the story up.</span>

<div id="review_572794132" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/572794132" />
    <a title="Beatriz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12372625-beatriz"><img alt="Beatriz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467433595p2/12372625.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/572794132?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatriz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatriz" href="/user/show/12372625-beatriz">Beatriz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12372625-beatriz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12372625-beatriz?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12372625-beatriz?shelf=best-books">best-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer572794132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18319964050516947863"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote><br/>“We’ve been through a lot over the years, but we made it, and we’ll continue to make it. Do you know why?” she asked.<br/>“Why?”<br/><br/>“Because infinity is forever, and that’s what you are to me. You’re my infinity, Mr. Black.”<br/>I turned to her and smiled as I traced her lips with my finger before brushing mine against them. “Forever us, baby. It’ll always be forever us.”<br/></blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>The perfect ending to one of my favorite series. It felt so great to witness how Connor and Ellery became parents. I knew that t</span>
  <span id="freeText18319964050516947863" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote><br />“We’ve been through a lot over the years, but we made it, and we’ll continue to make it. Do you know why?” she asked.<br />“Why?”<br /><br />“Because infinity is forever, and that’s what you are to me. You’re my infinity, Mr. Black.”<br />I turned to her and smiled as I traced her lips with my finger before brushing mine against them. “Forever us, baby. It’ll always be forever us.”<br /></blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />The perfect ending to one of my favorite series. It felt so great to witness how Connor and Ellery became parents. I knew that there would still be drama. Ellery was still the strong and independent woman she is from the beginning and Connor is still the over protective and controlling man he is. <br /><br />This story not only showed how Ellery and Connor surpassed all their challenges in being parents, it also showed that they are surrounded by loving friends and family. I love how Henri, Peyton, Denny, Dana, Mason and Landon became a big part of their lives. Not to mention the fact that they gave so much help in being there for Julia. <br /><br />There was this part of the book that I absolutely loved. Connor and Ellery never stopped loving each other no matter what happened and they always find a way to make up for lost time. The way they make love didn't differ from the moment they met and I absolutely admire that.<br /><br />The epilogue was great! I can't wait to read about Julia's novella. I hope we get a sneak at Collin and Hailey's love story as well.<br /><br /><b>10 INFINITY STARS!!!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="18319964050516947863" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385720830i/7211616.jpg' alt=' photo large-2_zpse8bc841f.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>The conclusion we've been all waiting for! The Black family sure knows how to make my heart swell!</b><br/><br/>Marriage add with newborn is very difficult to handle and Connor and Ellery showed us how to keep their family and friends be safe and loved. There are new challenges that they need to pass and together they will fight for those who will always makes them apart. I love how amazing parents they are. It truly melts my heart. I wish someday </span>
  <span id="freeText16864284404263893807" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Forever us baby, It'll always be forever us…"</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s144.photobucket.com/user/suyen02chubby/media/large-2_zpse8bc841f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385720830i/7211616.jpg" alt=" photo large-2_zpse8bc841f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>The conclusion we've been all waiting for! The Black family sure knows how to make my heart swell!</b><br><br>Marriage add with newborn is very difficult to handle and Connor and Ellery showed us how to keep their family and friends be safe and loved. There are new challenges that they need to pass and together they will fight for those who will always makes them apart. I love how amazing parents they are. It truly melts my heart. I wish someday I could have a husband like Connor Black, who will always be there to keep you safe. I'm so sad to read this ending because I will miss them. All those struggles and the sufferings they need to endure is all worth the fight! They've been through hell and worse but still they keep each other stronger. <br><br>It feels surreal to realize there will no more Connor Black who always made me cry since the first book. His love and devotion for his wife and kids are so amazing! Such a great man he is! <br><br><b>10 FOREVER STARS! - I will never forget this series for the rest of my life.</b></span>

It has little bit of everything and the author make sure that you feel the emotions that the characters are feeling, you will laugh, cry, some of the scenes will excite you, some will make your heart jump and most of all you feel the love. What i love about this book is the pacing it was not that fast nor slow, we get to see the adjustment that couples go through in the early stage of their married life and h</span>
  <span id="freeText4029190314037583386" style="display:none">Im out words on how to describe how freaking amazing the finale to the forever trilogy! It has little bit of everything and the author make sure that you feel the emotions that the characters are feeling, you will laugh, cry, some of the scenes will excite you, some will make your heart jump and most of all you feel the love. What i love about this book is the pacing it was not that fast nor slow, we get to see the adjustment that couples go through in the early stage of their married life and how to balance your time. The story also focuses in the importance of family, on having good friends and as a couple you should always be honest with each other. One more thing, the author got me in one of the scenes, it was well played. I've read a lot of series and only a few of them got the ending right but this one the author nailed iti! I couldn't ask for more, it was perfect.</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer802216385" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13625571783802042405">I'm really glad I finished this book. I always finish books I start, but I must say that this one was a bit painful to see through. Not because the plot lines were boring, or the plot lines were too intense or far-fetched (though they were). It was the writing style that made this so difficult to want to continue. The whole things is told in a very expositional way, with very little emotion behind it. Everything that happened felt very corny and clinical in the sense that I have read these exact</span>
  <span id="freeText13625571783802042405" style="display:none">I'm really glad I finished this book. I always finish books I start, but I must say that this one was a bit painful to see through. Not because the plot lines were boring, or the plot lines were too intense or far-fetched (though they were). It was the writing style that made this so difficult to want to continue. The whole things is told in a very expositional way, with very little emotion behind it. Everything that happened felt very corny and clinical in the sense that I have read these exact emotions and reactions over a hundred times in various other romance novels. In this case, this is a like the fast food version of a romance novel: it is filling but it makes you sick like an hour later and you hate yourself for going for it. While I can't say it is the worst thing I have ever read, it was just very bland and did not do what it was supposed to do for me. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13625571783802042405" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer757356149" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12780293780078903641">I absolutely loved the first two books in this series and patiently waited for this next one to be released. I was a little disappointed. Each obstacle that Ellery & Connor faced seemed to appear out of nowhere and was "fixed" rather quickly. I expected the issue with Ashlyn which was pretty prevelant in the first two books to be a larger part of this story but it was wrapped up pretty quickly. The ending was the most disappointing to me...the book jumped ahead in time several times and it was t</span>
  <span id="freeText12780293780078903641" style="display:none">I absolutely loved the first two books in this series and patiently waited for this next one to be released. I was a little disappointed. Each obstacle that Ellery &amp; Connor faced seemed to appear out of nowhere and was "fixed" rather quickly. I expected the issue with Ashlyn which was pretty prevelant in the first two books to be a larger part of this story but it was wrapped up pretty quickly. The ending was the most disappointing to me...the book jumped ahead in time several times and it was too far in the future. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NGOlM/tWdItCjBVdAEnGIn9DsJeDz9ddGO1gg3M6oX6grOGd1t2hFETJ2YFavSrFb2Q9Y1OamwTsEbdwmOCSMg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gTDvndDMTDijVuQQjsXpFUy5nF0bYAbWEWs1vE/ony0V/6sz/UeZp6UTKMzUMQXyXJ4Rqcs1So/ll+JPpDKsYQ==')})
  }
//]]>
